    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreaDate], [s].[CreaUser], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[IsStatus], [s].[IsTanim], [s].[LangId], [s].[LoginCount], [s].[ModDate], [s].[ModUser], [s].[Name], [s].[OrderNo], [s].[OrjId], [s].[ParentId], [s].[SpecType]

) AS [t]

    WHERE [s1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t1] ON [t].[OrjId] = [t1].[Id]
INNER JOIN (

    WHERE [l].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t2] ON [t].[LangId] = [t2].[Id]"
